window.forbes = window.forbes || {};
window.forbes.isAdvisor = templateType === 'advisor';// this file is external 3rd party code to initiate header prebidding which comes directly from Medianet
// https://forbesmedia.atlassian.net/browse/ADSS-77
/* eslint-disable no-underscore-dangle, camelcase */
window._mNHandle = window._mNHandle || {};
window._mNHandle.queue = window._mNHandle.queue || [];
window.forbes = window.forbes || {};
window.forbes.fastFetchMedianet = true;

// eslint-disable-next-line no-unused-vars
const medianet_versionId = '3121199';

(() => {
	const loadScript = (tagSrc) => {
		const scriptTag = document.createElement('script');
		const placeTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		scriptTag.type = 'text/javascript';
		scriptTag.async = true;
		scriptTag.src = tagSrc;
		placeTag.parentNode.insertBefore(scriptTag, placeTag);
	};

	const loadMedianetAd = () => {
		loadScript('https://contextual.media.net/dmedianet.js?cid=8CU2T3HV4&https=1');
	};

	const loadMedianetManagePrebid = (isMobile) => {
		window.mnjs = window.mnjs || {
			customerId: isMobile ? '8CU243I76' : '8CU4ZAPFY',
			domain: window.location.hostname,
			version: 1.0,
		};
		/* eslint-disable prefer-template */
		const mnjsEndpoint = 'https://warp.media.net/js/tags/clientag.js?'
			+ 'cid=' + window.mnjs.customerId
			+ '&dn=' + window.mnjs.domain
			+ '&version=' + window.mnjs.version;
		loadScript(mnjsEndpoint);
	};

	/**
	 * gets user agent from navigator info
	 * @param {String} ua user agent from navigator
	 * @param {String} isMobileAndroid for android devices
	 * @param {String} isMobileWindows for windows phone devices
	 * @returns a string representing the user agent
	 */
	const getIsMobile = (ua, isMobileAndroid, isMobileWindows) => ua.match(/iP(hone|od)/i)
		|| ua.match(/iPod/i)
		|| ua.match(/BlackBerry/i)
		|| isMobileAndroid
		|| isMobileWindows;

	const loadMedianetHeaderBidding = () => {
		if (window.forbes.isAdvisor) {
			loadScript('https://contextual.media.net/bidexchange.js?cid=8CU25AH4U');
		} else {
			const ua = navigator.userAgent;
			const isMobileAndroid = ua.match(/Android/i) && ua.match(/Mobile/i);
			const isMobileWindows = ua.match(/Nokia|NOKIA/i) && ua.match(/Symbian|Windows Phone/i);
			const isMobile = getIsMobile(ua, isMobileAndroid, isMobileWindows);
			loadMedianetManagePrebid(isMobile);
		}
	};

	/**
	 * check if the _swb_consent_ cookie is loaded
	 * @Todo make the ketch checks on the window so we can call them from there and make sure we dont
	 * lose time in the proccess
	 * we added ketch check to make sure we don't load medianet if the user is in the EU or China
	 * adding the checks here is a temporary solution.
	 * @returns boolean that represents if the cookie is loaded or not
	 */
	const checkConsentCookieLoaded = () => !!document.cookie.match(/_swb_consent_=/);

	/**
	 * get the _swb_consent_ cookie and url decode it to get it ready for parseing
	 * @returns String that has the ketch cookie value
	 */
	function getSwbCookieValue() {
		let cookieValue = false;
		if (!checkConsentCookieLoaded()) {
			return cookieValue;
		}

		const ketchCookieName = '_swb_consent_=';
		document.cookie.split(';').forEach((cookie) => {
			if (cookie.trim().startsWith(ketchCookieName)) {
				cookieValue = decodeURIComponent(cookie.split('=')[1]);
			}
		});

		return cookieValue;
	}

	/**
	 * get the cookie and parse it into json from base64 string
	 * @returns object that contains the consent details
	 */
	function getSwbCookie() {
		const ketchCookie = getSwbCookieValue();

		try {
			const cookieInfo = window.atob(ketchCookie);
			return JSON.parse(cookieInfo);
		} catch (error) {
			return {};
		}
	}

	/**
	 * Check if the user gave full consent.
	 * @returns If the user gave full consent.
	 */
	function userGaveFullConsent() {
		const userConsent = getSwbCookie();

		if (!userConsent.purposes) {
			return false;
		}

		const purposesKeys = Object.keys(userConsent.purposes);
		let userConsentPrefrences = true;

		// safety check for when the cookie is first intialized
		if (purposesKeys.length === 1) {
			return false;
		}

		purposesKeys.forEach((element) => {
			if (userConsent.purposes[element].allowed === 'false') {
				userConsentPrefrences = false;
			}
		});

		return userConsentPrefrences;
	}

	if (window.forbes.isEurope || window.forbes.isChina) {
		if (checkConsentCookieLoaded() && userGaveFullConsent()) {
			loadMedianetAd();
			loadMedianetHeaderBidding();
		}
	} else {
		loadMedianetAd();
		loadMedianetHeaderBidding();
	}
})();

const cookieIsSet = () => {
    if(document.cookie.split(';').find((cookie) => (cookie.indexOf(`fbs-zephr-access=`) > -1))) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
			event: 'analyticsEvent',
			'event category': 'Zephr',
			'event action': 'Sign In',
			'event label': 'General',
		});

        window.location.reload();
    } else {
        setTimeout(() => cookieIsSet(), 500);
    }
}


app.$$set({'onLogin': (function() {
    if (((window.Zephr || {}).utils || {}).callDataLayerUpdate) {
        window.Zephr.utils.callDataLayerUpdate().then(function () {
            cookieIsSet();
        });
    }
})});
</script><script type="text/javascript">
	const { href: url } = window.location;
	const isFDAPage = url.includes('/digital-assets/');

	function getCookieValue(cookies = '', cookieName) {
		return (cookies.split(';').find((cookie) => cookie.indexOf(`${cookieName}=`) > -1) || '').split('=')[1] || '';
	}

	async function registerFdaUser() {
		const zephrSessionID = getCookieValue(document.cookie, 'blaize_session');
		const data = {
			zephrSessionID,
			scopes: [0],
			action: 0,
		};

		try {
			const response = await fetch('https://fda.forbes.com/v2/extendedprofile', {
				method: 'POST',
				body: JSON.stringify(data),
				headers: {
					Accept: 'application/json',
					'Content-type': 'application/json',
				},
			});

			const results = await response.json();
			console.log('Registering FDA user::', results.message);
		} catch (error) {
			console.error('Error registering FDA user::', error);
		}
	}

	app.$$set({'onRegister': (function() {
    	window.dataLayer.push({
            event: 'analyticsEvent',
            'event category': 'Zephr',
            'event action': 'Register',
            'event label': 'General',
        });
		if (((window.Zephr || {}).utils || {}).callDataLayerUpdate) {
			window.Zephr.utils.callDataLayerUpdate().then(async function () {

				if (isFDAPage) {
					await registerFdaUser();
				}

				window.open(`https://account.forbes.com/onboarding`);
				window.location.reload();
			});
		}
	})});

let accountDataLayerEventObject = {
	event: 'analyticsEvent',
	'event category': 'Account',
	'event action': 'Account modal',
};

let registerFormFieldsAndButtons = {
	detailsFields: ['fname', 'lname', 'joblevel', 'jobfunction'],
	announcementsAndConsentCheckboxes: ['announcements', 'consent'],
	termsAndPolicyButtons: ['terms-of-service', 'privacy-policy'],
	emailAndPasswordFields: ['email-address', 'password-field', 'confirm-password-field'],
	socialNetworkButtons: ['google-auth', 'fb-auth', 'linkedin-auth'],
};

let waitForElmSignIn = (selector) => {
	return new Promise((resolve) => {
		if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
			return resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
		}

		const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
			if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
				resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
				observer.disconnect();
			}
		});

		observer.observe(document.body, {
			childList: true,
			subtree: true,
		});
	});
}

let prepareThirdStageEvents = () => {
	const personalDetailsFields = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-form-input');
	personalDetailsFields.forEach((field, fieldIndex) => {
		const detailsFieldName = registerFormFieldsAndButtons.detailsFields[fieldIndex] || '';

		field.addEventListener('click', () => {
			window.dataLayer.push({
				...accountDataLayerEventObject,
				'event label': `clicks-${detailsFieldName}`,
			});
		});
	});

	// register form - consent checkboxes
	const announcementsAndConsentCheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-form-checkbox');

	announcementsAndConsentCheckboxes.forEach((checkbox, checkboxIndex) => {
		let pushedEvent = false;
		const checkboxName = registerFormFieldsAndButtons.announcementsAndConsentCheckboxes[checkboxIndex] || '';

		checkbox.addEventListener('click', () => {
			if (!pushedEvent) {
				window.dataLayer.push({
					...accountDataLayerEventObject,
					'event label': `clicks-${checkboxName}`,
				});
				pushedEvent = true;
			}
		});
	});

	// register form - links
	const registerFormtermsAndPolicyButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-form-text > p > a');
	registerFormtermsAndPolicyButtons.forEach((button, buttonIndex) => {
		const buttonName = registerFormFieldsAndButtons.termsAndPolicyButtons[buttonIndex] || '';

		button.addEventListener('click', () => {
			window.dataLayer.push({
				...accountDataLayerEventObject,
				'event label': `clicks-${buttonName}`,
			});
		});
	});

	// register form - submit button
	const registrationFormContinueButton = document.querySelector('.zephr-registration-form-button[type="submit"]');
	registrationFormContinueButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
		const eventLabel = registrationFormContinueButton.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();

		window.dataLayer.push({
			...accountDataLayerEventObject,
			'event label': `clicks-${eventLabel}`,
		});
	});

	setUpProgressBarNavigation();
};

// second stage
let prepareSecondStageEvents = () => {
	// register form - email address, password, and confirm password input fields
	const emailAndPasswordFields = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-form-input');
	emailAndPasswordFields.forEach((field, fieldIndex) => {
		const fieldName = registerFormFieldsAndButtons.emailAndPasswordFields[fieldIndex] || '';

		field.addEventListener('click', () => {
			window.dataLayer.push({
				...accountDataLayerEventObject,
				'event label': `clicks-${fieldName}`,
			});
		});
	});

	// register form - continue button
	const registrationFormContinueButton = document.querySelector('.zephr-registration-form-button[type="submit"]');
	registrationFormContinueButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
		const eventLabel = registrationFormContinueButton.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();

		window.dataLayer.push({
			...accountDataLayerEventObject,
			'event label': `clicks-${eventLabel}`,
		});
	});

	setUpProgressBarNavigation();
	waitForElmSignIn('.zephr-registration-form-checkbox').then(() => prepareThirdStageEvents());
};

// first stage
let prepareFirstStageEvents = () => {
	// register form - email field
	const registerFormEmailField = document.querySelector('.zephr-registration-form-input');
	registerFormEmailField.addEventListener('click', () => {
		window.dataLayer.push({
			...accountDataLayerEventObject,
			'event label': 'clicks-email-address',
		});
	});

	// register form - continue with social networks
	const registrationFormSocialNetworkButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-form-social-sign-in-button');
	registrationFormSocialNetworkButtons.forEach((socialNetworkButton, socialNetworkButtonIndex) => {
		const socialNetworkButtonName = registerFormFieldsAndButtons.socialNetworkButtons[socialNetworkButtonIndex] || '';

		socialNetworkButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
			window.dataLayer.push({
				...accountDataLayerEventObject,
				'event label': `clicks-${socialNetworkButtonName}`,
			});
		});
	});

	// register form - sign up/in or continue button
	const registrationFormSubmitButton = document.querySelector('.zephr-registration-form-button[type="submit"]');
	registrationFormSubmitButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
		window.dataLayer.push({
			...accountDataLayerEventObject,
			'event label': 'clicks-signin-or-register',
		});
	});

	waitForElmSignIn('.zephr-registration-form-password-progress').then(() => prepareSecondStageEvents());
	waitForElmSignIn('.zephr-form-link').then(() => prepareSecondStageEvents());
};

const setUpProgressBarNavigation = () => {
	const progressBarSteps = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-progress-bar-step');
	progressBarSteps.forEach((step) => {
		step.addEventListener('click', () => {
			const stepName = step.textContent.trim();

			if (stepName === 'EMAIL') {
				waitForElmSignIn('.zephr-registration-form-divider-container').then(() => prepareFirstStageEvents());
			} else if (stepName === 'PASSWORD') {
				waitForElmSignIn('.zephr-registration-form-password-progress').then(() => prepareSecondStageEvents());
			} else if (stepName === 'DETAILS') {
				waitForElmSignIn('.zephr-registration-form-checkbox').then(() => prepareThirdStageEvents());
			}
		});
	});
}

const registerFormOpened = function(mutationsList, observer) {
	mutationsList.forEach((mutation) => {
		if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'class') {
			window.dataLayer.push({
				...accountDataLayerEventObject,
				'event label': 'shown',
			});

			prepareFirstStageEvents();
			bodyObserver.disconnect();
		}
	});
};

const bodyObserver = new MutationObserver(registerFormOpened);

bodyObserver.observe(document.body, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class'] });

function waitForElmDisplayName(selector) {
	return new Promise((resolve) => {
		if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
			return resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
		}

		const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
			if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
				resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
				observer.disconnect();
			}
		});

		observer.observe(document.body, {
			childList: true,
			subtree: true,
		});
	});
}

let displayName;
let lastName;
let displayNameString = '';
let firstNameString = '';
let lastNameString = '';

waitForElmDisplayName('[placeholder="First Name"]').then((firstName) => {
	lastName = document.querySelector('[placeholder="Last Name"]');
	displayName = document.querySelector('[placeholder="Display Name"]');
	displayName.style.display = 'none';

	firstName.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
		firstNameString = e.target.value;
		displayNameString = firstNameString + lastNameString;
		displayName.value = displayNameString;
		displayName.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', {
			view: window,
			bubbles: true,
			cancelable: true,
		}));
	});

	lastName.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
		lastNameString = ` ${e.target.value.charAt(0)}`;
		displayNameString = firstNameString + lastNameString;
		displayName.value = displayNameString;
		displayName.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', {
			view: window,
			bubbles: true,
			cancelable: true,
		}));
	});
});

    const emailRegExp = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;

    function setEmailFieldValidation(emailInput) {
    	const submitButton = emailInput.closest('form.zephr-registration-form, .zephr-payment-form').querySelector('.zephr-registration-form-button, .zephr-payment-form-button');
    	emailInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
    		submitButton.disabled = !emailRegExp.test(emailInput.value);
    	});
    }

    const emailFieldObserver = new MutationObserver((mutationsList) => {
    	mutationsList.forEach((mutation) => {
    		if (mutation.type === 'childList' && mutation.addedNodes.length) {
    			mutation.addedNodes.forEach((node) => {
    				const emailFieldsClasses = ['zephr-registration-form-input-email', 'zephr-payment-form-input-email'];
    				if (node.classList && emailFieldsClasses.some((emailFieldClass) => node.classList.contains(emailFieldClass))) {
    					setEmailFieldValidation(node);
    				}
    			});
    		}
    	});
    });

    emailFieldObserver.observe(document.body, {
    	childList: true,
    	subtree: true,
    });

    const allEmailFields = document.querySelectorAll('.zephr-registration-form-input-email, .zephr-payment-form-input-email');

    allEmailFields.forEach((emailField) => {
    	setEmailFieldValidation(emailField);
    });
